I was able to get in and out in less than an hour.  The SSA employee was friendly, knowledgeable, and courteous.  He worked at window number 3. The key is to get there  early  and have all your documents, i.e. ID,SS card etc.  The only negative was the long line to get to the service window.< /review>

< Review>
The people who work here are friendly and polite. The wait time can be quite long, but this will vary; you may want to plan for at least 4 hours. You will need to bring your S.S. Card the 1st time; after that you'll be in the system. You will need to bring your own notebook if you want anything to write on because they won't provide you with a piece of paper to use. It's best to have your questions written down before you go. They do have a booklet that has some of the answers on S.S. I lost a $40 sweathirt in this office (I dropped it) and went back to look for it in 1 hour, but it was gone and the security officers couldn't find it. This place is at risk for theft so take care with what you bring.</Review>

Showed up at 0830, there was already a line in front of the building. If you don‚Äôt have an appointment better show up early. Security comes out about 0845 to give a brief. I was there for a name change, it went smoothly. Security is nice and the woman who helped me was very nice. Another reviewer complained about having her purse searched. <Rate>3< /Rate><review>The Skillets Diner is new to Bakersfield and on Sunday May 26, we tried out their breakfast.

On the positive side, we found the coffee delicious and the atmosphere was pleasant. While we waited for our meals, our drinks were refilled on a very frequent basis. My wife ordered the French toast with an egg and bacon on the side. She remarked how everything was delicious. I ordered the Denver omelet with hashbrowns, a side of bacon and rye toast. The omelette was cooked to my satisfaction and the hash browns and bacon were done as asked. Instead of regular rye toast, I was presented with Marble Rye, a pleasant surprise. All in all, everything on the plate was very good.

On the negative side, service was very slow, but that‚Äôs to be expected with a new opening. It took over 45 minutes from the time we were seated before we received our meals. During this time, I noticed several people who had been waiting, left before they were seated. Perhaps the empty area in the middle of the establishment will soon be utilized in the future to accommodate more people.

We suspect that once the kinks are worked out, the Skillets Diner will be a pleasing experience for many years to come. We will certainly be back.</review><Pics>None< /Pics><resp>None<//resp><gmapID>0x80ea438dc0fae2d9:0x3722d5e86d45c078<//gmapID></record></dataset><record>

<Rating>4</Rating><Review>WOW this place has the kindest service ever. The guy taking your order was so sweet and polite... seriously never have I been talked to in such a courteous manner. He gave us recommendations and so we got the baby back ribs (just the ribs, I think it's 1 lb) with the sides mac n cheese, coleslaw and corn bread. The mac n cheese was DELICIOUS. Usually I don't like eating too much mac n cheese but for some reason, something is extra appealing about theirs. The coleslaw was great too - my bf said the coleslaw was his favorite out of the side dishes. I got the cornbread because of the yelp reviews and it didn't disappoint. Now onto the ribs, the only problem I had with it was the the ribs on the side were extra dry. It wasn't even pleasant at all to eat. But the ribs in the middle were cooked to perfection. If all the ribs tasted like the ones in the middle, then this place would've gotten 5 stars from me. Also, don't forget to use the sauces they provide! It makes the ribs taste 10000x better. Parking was easy for me since I came right before it closed, but I could see it being potentially difficult during the day. Also, I thought the location was kinda sketch at first since it's all homes surrounding it but it turns out to be a nice surprise!</Review>< user>

<Review>This place was so refreshing and nice to come to on Sunday superbowl, when you don't like all of the hype of a big crowded and loud restaurant and just wanna relax. It looks pretty basic on the outside first time seeing it, but it won't disappoint. The service was nice and friendly, and food came really quick. Nice classic BBQ menu with all the classic sides, without the lines, waits, crowd and fuss. The food is BOMB, and hits the spot if your craving that classic charred BBQ flavor.

The meat is not overly cooked and tough, and is fall off the bone. The BBQ beans are peeerfect, I'd say the cornbread was different as it wasn't sweet at all like traditionally flavored corn bread but it's still good. Tried everything from what we ordered and it was all good. Mmmhmmm. :) Will be coming back. No cons here.< /Review>< pics>

<Rating>5</Rating><text>Overall, two thumbs and four paws up!

If you like Pet Food Express, or any other store that feels a lot less like a typical Petco/Petsmart-style huge commercial venture, with gigantic stores and staff that knows very little about what they do, then Unleashed by Petco is for you.

Their product selection is a little less comprehensive than a full-blown Petco, and I think Pet Food Express is far better at stocking well-priced, well-thought-out, and great quality apparel-type items (I always get compliments on my dog's raincoat, which is easily the best thing I never even thought existed, before I saw it at PFE, and even has a functional hood).

That being said, these little stores always seem very thoughtfully stocked, and it's hard to leave this one without a couple large armloads of good quality food (especially if you like the high-quality, grain-free, and high-protein varieties), and necessities that larger stores or other small stores simply don't stock.

This particular store is staffed by really friendly people, and if you own a medium or large dog, you can expect to actually find things here for them, like the dreaded doggie diapers you need to assist your older friend, a large variety of high-quality treats, especially long-lasting and/or puzzle types, and a great selection of hygiene products for fur, skin, teeth, and first aid.  They also carry a basic, but well-chosen and comprehensive range of supplements.  Last but hardly least, this tiny location has a tag engraver, and, of course, the tags to go with it.</text></record>

< Review>
This business was decent years a couple of years ago when I started coming. Over the years it has just completely fallen downhill. You'd assume with COVID and all that they would want the business, but the ladies who work here continue to be more lazy, unprofessional, and just rude (especially the Hispanic worker who does the manicures). Instead of setting you an appointment they'll make excuse for you to come on in and see if they're busy. So of course when you do arrive, they have 'no openings,' even though it's completely dead.
